===== TEMPLATE 23 (sent 17x | properties: Cozy Lakefront Home w/ Game Room, Hot Tub, Fire Pit, & Boats)
Hey Dania, 



We’re so excited to host your stay in the beautiful Poconos! Below you will find check-in instructions as well as some general Information about the home.



Check-in: Aug 2, 2024 at  4:00 PM

Check-out: Aug 4, 2024 at 11:00 AM





We have guests checking in on Aug 4, 2024, so we ask that you please adhere to the 11:00 AM checkout time. Thanks for your understanding!



Arriving at the community: 



Penn Estates is a gated community with 2 entrances. ALL GUESTS MUST CHECK IN AT THE MAIN GATE , LOCATED AT: 



525 Penn Estates Dr, East Stroudsburg PA, 18301. 



Drive up to gate via the right-side "Visitors" lane, and contact the gatestaff through the button on the machine. The registered guest will need to provide a valid drivers license at check-in. 



Upon check-in you will receive a printed gate pass, which can be used to enter both the front and back gates for the duration of your stay. 



Entry Door Lock:

Your door code is 4867. 



- To unlock the door from the outside, enter the code and press the enter button. Turn the knob counter-clockwise. 

- To lock the door from the outside, enter the code and press the enter button. Turn the knob clockwise. 





Parking:

- Driveway is gravel and on a hill. Be careful and drive slowly up and down the driveway. You can fit up to 5 cars.



DO NOT PARK IN THE STREET.



Wifi:



Name: Lakehouse Wifi

Password: relax449



Safety:

- Fire Extinguisher is under the sink.

- First Aid Kit is in the labeled cabinet in the kitchen.

- Life Jackets for Kayaks are located in the downstairs closet.

- Call 911 for any other emergencies and please contact us immediately.



Temperature:

- Each room has its own thermostat for heat that can be adjusted manually with the controls. 

- Window AC units are controlled individually in each room.

- Hot water heater holds 50 gallons. Please space bath and showers accordingly.





FIREPLACE:

- Turning On: The gas fireplace is turned on using the thermostat to the right of the fireplace. Push the bottom left tab to the heat (left) position. The fireplace will turn on in a few seconds. 



- Turning Off: Push the bottom left tab to the off (right) position. 



HOT TUB: 

- Hot tub is always on and ready to use. 

- Feel free to adjust the temperature as desired using the controls. 

- NO FOOD OR DRINKS IN HOT TUB!

- Please be sure to keep hot tub lid closed when not in use. 

– Please make sure to wash off any lotions or hair gels prior to entering the hot tub, as these will cause chemical imbalances in the water.  – There are individual plastic cups with chlorine powder in them in the cabinet above the kitchen microwave. Drop one of these into the tub after each use to ensure the hot tub stays fresh for your next use.It’s 





TV:

- Watch TV via LG Internet TV: Use LG remote to turn on TV (it takes 5 secs to come up). Then navigate to the LG TV app, Netflix, or another streaming service of your choice.



QUIET HOURS:

- 11pm to 7am. Please be respectful to neighbors at all times.



TRASH:

All trash should be placed in the bins just outside the garage door, they are mixed use trash and recycling so either works. It is picked up between monday morning and tuesday night directly from where they are, so no need to bring anything to the street. If they are filled up and you are checking out prior to pick up, just place your bags next to the bins and we will take care of it from there.



GUESTS &amp; DELIVERIES: 



All guests must be noted on the registration form. Guests who are not on the form will be denied entry at the gate. 



To allow a food, Uber, or any other delivery driver through the gate, you must send a message via Airbnb, and we will call them into the gate. Gatehouse staff will not allow any driver through without a regstration form or a delivery call in. 



Our general store inside the .community is Archie's Corner (www.archiescorner.com) and is available for food and any last minute needs at 443 Penn Estates drive, next to the pools and community center. We recommend the breakfast sandwich, Italian Hero, and chicken fingers!



Check-out: 11am



The cleaning fee is for basic whole house cleaning. Anything out of ordinary (such as excessive trash, unremovable stains, etc) will incur guests extra cleaning fees as per the rental agreement.



- If you have any questions/ issues, feel free to contact me. I will try my best to make your stay as comfortable and pleasant as possible. Enjoy your stay and have a wonderful vacation!



Thank you!

Feliks

732-213-8571

===== TEMPLATE 37 (sent 12x | properties: Cozy Lakefront Home w/ Game Room, Hot Tub, Fire Pit, & Boats)
Hey Baseer, 



We’re so excited to host your stay in the beautiful Poconos! Below you will find check-in instructions as well as some general Information about the home.



Check-in: Apr 23, 2025 at  4:00 PM

Check-out: Apr 25, 2025 at 11:00 AM





We have guests checking in on Apr 25, 2025, so we ask that you please adhere to the 11:00 AM checkout time. Thanks for your understanding!



Arriving at the community: 



Penn Estates is a gated community with 2 entrances. ALL GUESTS MUST CHECK IN AT THE MAIN GATE , LOCATED AT: 



525 Penn Estates Dr, East Stroudsburg PA, 18301. 



Drive up to gate via the right-side "Visitors" lane, and contact the gatestaff through the button on the machine. The registered guest will need to provide a valid drivers license at check-in. 



Upon check-in you will receive a printed gate pass, which can be used to enter both the front and back gates for the duration of your stay. 



Entry Door Lock:

Your door code is 4867. 



- To unlock the door from the outside, enter the code and press the enter button. Turn the knob counter-clockwise. 

- To lock the door from the outside, enter the code and press the enter button. Turn the knob clockwise. 





Parking:

- Driveway is gravel and on a hill. Be careful and drive slowly up and down the driveway. You can fit up to 5 cars.



DO NOT PARK IN THE STREET.



Wifi:



Name: Lakehouse Wifi

Password: relax449



Safety:

- Fire Extinguisher is under the sink.

- First Aid Kit is in the labeled cabinet in the kitchen.

- Life Jackets for Kayaks are located in the downstairs closet.

- Call 911 for any other emergencies and please contact us immediately.



Temperature:

- Each room has its own thermostat for heat that can be adjusted manually with the controls. 

- Window AC units are controlled individually in each room.

- Hot water heater holds 50 gallons. Please space bath and showers accordingly.





FIREPLACE:

- Turning On: The gas fireplace is turned on using the thermostat to the right of the fireplace. Push the bottom left tab to the heat (left) position. The fireplace will turn on in a few seconds. 



- Turning Off: Push the bottom left tab to the off (right) position. 



HOT TUB: 

- Hot tub is always on and ready to use. 

- Feel free to adjust the temperature as desired using the controls. 

- NO FOOD OR DRINKS IN HOT TUB!

- Please be sure to keep hot tub lid closed when not in use. 

– Please make sure to wash off any lotions or hair gels prior to entering the hot tub, as these will cause chemical imbalances in the water.  – There are individual plastic cups with chlorine powder in them in the cabinet above the kitchen microwave. Drop one of these into the tub after each use to ensure the hot tub stays fresh for your next use.It’s 





TV:

- Watch TV via LG Internet TV: Use LG remote to turn on TV (it takes 5 secs to come up). Then navigate to the LG TV app, Netflix, or another streaming service of your choice.



QUIET HOURS:

- 11pm to 7am. Please be respectful to neighbors at all times.



TRASH:

All trash should be placed in the bins just outside the garage door, they are mixed use trash and recycling so either works. It is picked up between monday morning and tuesday night directly from where they are, so no need to bring anything to the street. If they are filled up and you are checking out prior to pick up, just place your bags next to the bins and we will take care of it from there.



GUESTS &amp; DELIVERIES: 



All guests must be noted on the registration form. Guests who are not on the form will be denied entry at the gate. 



To allow a food, Uber, or any other delivery driver through the gate, you must send a message via Airbnb, and we will call them into the gate. Gatehouse staff will not allow any driver through without a regstration form or a delivery call in. 



Our general store inside the .community is Archie's Corner (www.archiescorner.com) and is available for food and any last minute needs at 443 Penn Estates drive, next to the pools and community center. We recommend the breakfast sandwich, Italian Hero, and chicken fingers!



Check-out: 11am



The cleaning fee is for basic whole house cleaning. Anything out of ordinary (such as excessive trash, unremovable stains, etc) will incur guests extra cleaning fees as per the rental agreement.



- If you have any questions/ issues, feel free to contact me. I will try my best to make your stay as comfortable and pleasant as possible. Enjoy your stay and have a wonderful vacation!



Thank you!

Feliks

732-213-8571

Arriving at the community: 



Penn Estates is a gated community with 2 entrances. ALL GUESTS MUST CHECK IN AT THE MAIN GATE , LOCATED AT: 



525 Penn Estates Dr, East Stroudsburg PA, 18301



This is at Penn Estates Dr and Hallet Rd. Make sure your directions don’t take you through the back gate to get there (Penn Estates Dr and Cranburry Rd) as entry will not be permitted that way.



Drive up to gate via the right-side "Visitors" lane, and contact the gatestaff through the button on the machine. The registered guest will need to provide a valid drivers license at check-in. 



Upon check-in you will receive a printed gate pass, which can be used to enter both the front and back gates for the duration of your stay.



Do not share gate passes or sneak additional vehicles or guests that haven’t been registered. I can not emohasize this enough: they have automatic cameras, security will catch you, and you will recieve an unreasonably high citation. Let’s follow the rules and avoid this please!



Entry Door Lock:

- There is a lock box on the ground floor door under the deck. Use  code 8550 to unlock the box and access the door key. If you have trouble, you want to lock halfway before closing so the little latch is partially out, firmly slide the door closed, and lock the rest of the way.



Please return the key to the lockbox anytime you leave the house and venture out. This will ensure you don’t lock yourself out. Losing the key will result in a $50 replacement fee which will be deducted from your deposit.





Parking:

- Driveway is on a hill. Be careful and drive slowly up and down the driveway. You can fit up to 5 cars in a row.



DO NOT PARK IN THE STREET.



Wifi:



Name: The Chalet

Password: relax475



Safety:

- Fire Extinguisher is under the sink.

- First Aid Kit is in the labeled cabinet in the kitchen.

- Life Jackets for Kayaks are located in the upstairs closet.

- Call 911 for any other emergencies and please contact us immediately.



Temperature:

- Each room has its own thermostat for heat that can be adjusted manually with the controls. 

- All rooms are equiped with air conditioning. Please use the white remote on the wall to turn it on and set the desired temperature. In order for the system to work, all rooms must be set to COOL. If one of the rooms is set to HEAT, while the others are set to cool, the system will not function and will display an error message. You can confirm the setting is correct when you see the snowflake icon on the remote LCD screen. 



- Hot water heater holds 50 gallons. Please space bath and showers accordingly.





FIREPLACE:

- Turning On: The gas fireplace is turned on using the small black remote. Press the button once (you will hear a beep) to turn it on. Fire will start automatically within 60 seconds after the beep.

- Turning Off: Press the button once. You will hear two beeps and the fire will turn off.



HOT TUB: 

- Hot tub is always on and ready to use. 

- Feel free to adjust the temperature as desired using the controls. 

- NO FOOD OR DRINKS IN HOT TUB!

- Please be sure to keep hot tub lid closed when not in use. 

– Please make sure to wash off any lotions or hair gels prior to entering the hot tub, as these will cause chemical imbalances in the water.  – There are individual plastic cups with chlorine powder in them in the cabinet above the kitchen microwave. Drop one of these into the tub after each use to ensure the hot tub stays fresh for your next use.



SAUNA:

The sauna is an infrared sauna, that opperates on a 90 minute timer. It takes about 30-45 minutes to get up to a good temperature (most people prefer 120-140), though a bit longer if it is cold outside. Infrared sauna works by heating your body directly, so it may not feel super hot when you first enter but will quickly heat you up once inside. 



TV:

- Watch TV via LG Internet TV: Use LG remote to turn on TV (it takes 5 secs to come up). Then navigate to the LG TV app, Netflix, or another streaming service of your choice.



COMMUNITY AMENITIES:

•You will need the amenity passes to use these, which you will find hanging on the oars by the entrance. It is always a total of 12 of these, please be very careful not to lose them as they are specific to the home and a $175 replacement fee.

• There are two community pools (open memorial day weekend till  labor day weekend) located at 443 Penn Estates Dr, next to the Archies Corner community store.﻿ The daily pool hours are 11:00 am – 7:00 pm swim at your own risk (not always lifeguards), pending weather conditions.

• Athletic fields and courts are right next to the pools and community center as well.

• ﻿There is also a swimmable beach lake. If you exit out the door and turn left you just go straight and cant miss the beach lake area on your left, about a 12 min walk or 1min drive from the home. You should also bring the amenity passes mentioned above just in case they check at the lake.



CANOES and KAYAKS:

(the red one with 81C on the label, rack no. TL4 on the bottom). Oars and a kayak are on the front of the home and life jackets are in the upstairs closet. Please make sure to return all after use.

Temperature:

- Each room has its own thermostat for heat that can be adjusted manually with the controls. 

- All rooms are equiped with air conditioning. Please use the white remote on the wall to turn it on and set the desired temperature. In order for the system to work, all rooms must be set to COOL. If one of the rooms is set to HEAT, while the others are set to cool, the system will not function and will display an error message. You can confirm the setting is correct when you see the snowflake icon on the remote LCD screen. 



- Hot water heater holds 50 gallons. Please space bath and showers accordingly.





FIREPLACE:

- Turning On: The gas fireplace is turned on using the small black remote. Press the button once (you will hear a beep) to turn it on. Fire will start automatically within 60 seconds after the beep.

- Turning Off: Press the button once. You will hear two beeps and the fire will turn off.



HOT TUB: 

- Hot tub is always on and ready to use. 

- Feel free to adjust the temperature as desired using the controls. 

- NO FOOD OR DRINKS IN HOT TUB!

- Please be sure to keep hot tub lid closed when not in use. 

– Please make sure to wash off any lotions or hair gels prior to entering the hot tub, as these will cause chemical imbalances in the water.  – There are individual plastic cups with chlorine powder in them in the cabinet above the kitchen microwave. Drop one of these into the tub after each use to ensure the hot tub stays fresh for your next use.



SAUNA:

The sauna is an infrared sauna, that opperates on a 90 minute timer. It takes about 30-45 minutes to get up to a good temperature (most people prefer 120-140), though a bit longer if it is cold outside. Infrared sauna works by heating your body directly, so it may not feel super hot when you first enter but will quickly heat you up once inside. 



TV:

- Watch TV via LG Internet TV: Use LG remote to turn on TV (it takes 5 secs to come up). Then navigate to the LG TV app, Netflix, or another streaming service of your choice.



POOLS:

There are two community pools located at 443 Penn Estates Dr, next to the Archies Corner community store. You will need the amenity passes to use them, which you will find hanging on the oar by the entrance. It is always a total of 12 of these, please be very careful not to lose them as they are specific to the home and a $75 replacement fee. The daily pool hours are 11:00 am – 7:00 pm swim at your own risk (not always lifeguards), pending weather conditions.



CANOES and KAYAKS:

If you exit the home and turn right, the easement entrance to the lake is two homes down on your left. We have a canoe ready for you on a rack at the lake. (the red one with 81C on the label, rack no. TL4 on the bottom). Oars and a kayak are on the front of the home and life jackets are in the upstairs closet. Please make sure to return all after use.



BEACH LAKE:

There is also a swimmable beach lake. If you exit out the door and turn left you just go straight and cant miss the beach lake area on your left, about a 12 min walk or 1min drive from the home. You should also bring the amenity passes mentioned above just in case they check at the lake.



QUIET HOURS:

- 11pm to 7am. Please be respectful to neighbors at all times.



TRASH:

All trash should be placed in the bins just outside the garage door, they are mixed use trash and recycling so either works. It is picked up between monday morning and tuesday night directly from where they are, so no need to bring anything to the street. If they are filled up and you are checking out prior to pick up, just place your bags next to the bins and we will take care of it from there.



GUESTS &amp; DELIVERIES: 



All guests must be noted on the registration form. Guests who are not on the form will be denied entry at the gate. 



To allow a food, Uber, or any other delivery driver through the gate, you must send a message via Airbnb, and we will call them into the gate. Gatehouse staff will not allow any driver through without a regstration form or a delivery call in. 



Our general store inside the .community is Archie's Corner (www.archiescorner.com) and is available for food and any last minute needs at 443 Penn Estates drive, next to the pools and community center. We recommend the breakfast sandwich, Italian Hero, and chicken fingers!



Check-out: 11am



The cleaning fee is for basic whole house cleaning. Anything out of ordinary (such as excessive trash, unremovable stains, etc) will incur guests extra cleaning fees as per the rental agreement.



- If you have any questions/ issues, feel free to contact me. I will try my best to make your stay as comfortable and pleasant as possible. Enjoy your stay and have a wonderful vacation!



Thank you!

Arriving at the community: 



Penn Estates is a gated community with 2 entrances. ALL GUESTS MUST CHECK IN AT THE MAIN GATE , LOCATED AT: 



525 Penn Estates Dr, East Stroudsburg PA, 18301. 



This is at Penn Estates Dr and Hallet Rd. Make sure your directions don’t take you through the back gate to get there (Penn Estates Dr and Cranburry Rd) as entry will not be permitted that way.



Drive up to gate via the right-side "Visitors" lane, and contact the gatestaff through the button on the machine. The registered guest will need to provide a valid drivers license at check-in. 



Upon check-in you will receive a printed gate pass, which can be used to enter both the front and back gates for the duration of your stay. 



Do not share gate passes or sneak additional vehicles or guests that haven’t been registered. I can not emohasize this enough: they have automatic cameras, security will catch you, and you will recieve an unreasonably high citation. Let’s follow the rules and avoid this please!



Entry Door Lock: 8550



- To unlock from outside: Tap the Yale button on the door lock. A keypad will appear. Use the pin provided above, and hit “✔︎” to submit the code.



To lock from outside: Tap the "Yale" logo. Make sure it is locked.



Parking:

- Driveway is h-shaped and is on a hill. Be careful and drive slowly up and down the driveway. You can fit up to 6 cars.



DO NOT PARK IN THE STREET.



Wifi:



Name: Lakeside 

Password:  relax484



GUESTS &amp; DELIVERIES: 



All guests must be noted on the registration form. Guests who are not on the form will be denied entry at the gate. 



To allow a food, Uber, or any other delivery driver through the gate, you must send a message via airbnb, and we will submit it into the gate. Gatehouse staff will not allow any driver through without a regstration form or a delivery registration. 



Our general store inside the community is Archie's Corner (www.archiescorner.com) and is available for food and any last minute needs at 443 Penn Estates drive, next to the pools and community center. We recommend the breakfast sandwich, Italian Hero, and chicken fingers!



HOT TUB: 

- Hot tub is always on and ready to use. 

- Feel free to adjust the temperature as desired using the controls. 

- NO FOOD OR DRINKS IN HOT TUB!

- Please be sure to keep hot tub lid closed when not in use. 

– Please make sure to wash off any lotions or hair gels prior to entering the hot tub, as these will cause chemical imbalances in the water.  – There are individual plastic cups with chlorine powder in them in the cabinet above the kitchen microwave. Drop one of these into the tub after each use to ensure the hot tub stays fresh for your next use.It’s 





Safety:

- Fire Extinguisher is under the sink.

- First Aid Kit is in the labeled cabinet in the kitchen.

- Life Jackets for Kayaks are located in the upstairs closet.

- Call 911 for any other emergencies and please contact us immediately.



Temperature:

- All bedrooms use a split unit AC system, and the living room has its own additional split unit AC, these also work as a heating system. Additional heat can be turned on using the thermostats for baseboard heat, but this a backup and should not be necessary as the split unit system is very powerful. Use the remotes to turn on. Please be advised all units must be switched to the same mode (cool vs heat) for them to work. If you receive an error please ensure that is the case. The cool icon (snowflake) looks very similar to the heat icon (sun), so always good to double check!



- Hot water heater holds 50 gallons. Please space bath and showers accordingly.



FIREPLACE:

- The fireplace is controlled with dial on the front/center of the unit. To turn on the flame simply turn counterclockwise 1-5. To turn off, turn the dial clockwise one to the pilot position. Be careful not to turn too far into the off position as this will turn off the pilot light, which should stay on at all times. 



COMMUNITY AMENITIES:

•You will need the amenity passes to use these, which you will find hanging on the oars by the entrance. It is always a total of 12 of these, please be very careful not to lose them as they are specific to the home and a $175 replacement fee.

• There are two community pools (open memorial day weekend till  labor day weekend) located at 443 Penn Estates Dr, next to the Archies Corner community store.﻿ The daily pool hours are 11:00 am – 7:00 pm swim at your own risk (not always lifeguards), pending weather conditions.

• Athletic fields and courts are right next to the pools and community center as well.

• ﻿There is an additional a swimmable beach lake. If you exit out the door and turn right you just go straight and cant miss the beach lake area on your left, about a 12 min walk or 1min drive from the home. You should also bring the amenity passes mentioned above just in case they check at the lake.



TV:

- Watch TV via LG Internet TV: Use LG remote to turn on TV (it takes 5 secs to come up). Then navigate to the LG TV app, Netflix, or another streaming service of your choice.



QUIET HOURS:

- 11pm to 7am. Please be respectful to neighbors at all times.



TRASH:

It is picked up between monday morning and tuesday night directly from where they are, so no need to bring anything to the street. If they are filled up and you are checking out prior to pick up, just place your bags next to the bins and we will take care of it from there.

===== TEMPLATE 84 (sent 6x | properties: Cozy Lakefront Home w/ Game Room, Hot Tub, Fire Pit, & Boats)
Hey Michelle, 



We’re so excited to host your stay in the beautiful Poconos! Below you will find check-in instructions as well as some general Information about the home.



Check-in: Sep 13, 2024 at  4:00 PM

Check-out: Sep 15, 2024 at 11:00 AM





We have guests checking in on Sep 15, 2024, so we ask that you please adhere to the 11:00 AM checkout time. Thanks for your understanding!



Arriving at the community: 



Penn Estates is a gated community with 2 entrances. ALL GUESTS MUST CHECK IN AT THE MAIN GATE , LOCATED AT: 



525 Penn Estates Dr, East Stroudsburg PA, 18301. 



Drive up to gate via the right-side "Visitors" lane, and contact the gatestaff through the button on the machine. The registered guest will need to provide a valid drivers license at check-in. 



Upon check-in you will receive a printed gate pass, which can be used to enter both the front and back gates for the duration of your stay. 



Entry Door Lock:

Your door code is 4867. 



- To unlock the door from the outside, enter the code and press the enter button. Turn the knob counter-clockwise. 

- To lock the door from the outside, enter the code and press the enter button. Turn the knob clockwise. 





Parking:

- Driveway is gravel and on a hill. Be careful and drive slowly up and down the driveway. You can fit up to 5 cars.



DO NOT PARK IN THE STREET.



Wifi:



Name: Lakehouse Wifi

Password: relax449



Safety:

- Fire Extinguisher is under the sink.

- First Aid Kit is in the labeled cabinet in the kitchen.

- Life Jackets for Kayaks are located in the downstairs closet.

- Call 911 for any other emergencies and please contact us immediately.



Temperature:

- Each room has its own thermostat for heat that can be adjusted manually with the controls. 

- Window AC units are controlled individually in each room.

- Hot water heater holds 50 gallons. Please space bath and showers accordingly.





FIREPLACE:

- Turning On: The gas fireplace is turned on using the thermostat to the right of the fireplace. Push the bottom left tab to the heat (left) position. The fireplace will turn on in a few seconds. 



- Turning Off: Push the bottom left tab to the off (right) position. 



HOT TUB: 

- Hot tub is always on and ready to use. 

- Feel free to adjust the temperature as desired using the controls. 

- NO FOOD OR DRINKS IN HOT TUB!

- Please be sure to keep hot tub lid closed when not in use. 

– Please make sure to wash off any lotions or hair gels prior to entering the hot tub, as these will cause chemical imbalances in the water.  – There are individual plastic cups with chlorine powder in them in the cabinet above the kitchen microwave. Drop one of these into the tub after each use to ensure the hot tub stays fresh for your next use.It’s 





TV:

- Watch TV via LG Internet TV: Use LG remote to turn on TV (it takes 5 secs to come up). Then navigate to the LG TV app, Netflix, or another streaming service of your choice.



QUIET HOURS:

- 11pm to 7am. Please be respectful to neighbors at all times.



TRASH:

All trash should be placed in the bins just outside the garage door, they are mixed use trash and recycling so either works. It is picked up between monday morning and tuesday night directly from where they are, so no need to bring anything to the street. If they are filled up and you are checking out prior to pick up, just place your bags next to the bins and we will take care of it from there.



GUESTS &amp; DELIVERIES: 



All guests must be noted on the registration form. Guests who are not on the form will be denied entry at the gate. 



To allow a food, Uber, or any other delivery driver through the gate, you must send a message via Airbnb, and we will call them into the gate. Gatehouse staff will not allow any driver through without a regstration form or a delivery call in. 



Our general store inside the .community is Archie's Corner (www.archiescorner.com) and is available for food and any last minute needs at 443 Penn Estates drive, next to the pools and community center. We recommend the breakfast sandwich, Italian Hero, and chicken fingers!



Check-out: 11am



The cleaning fee is for basic whole house cleaning. Anything out of ordinary (such as excessive trash, unremovable stains, etc) will incur guests extra cleaning fees as per the rental agreement.



- If you have any questions/ issues, feel free to contact me. I will try my best to make your stay as comfortable and pleasant as possible. Enjoy your stay and have a wonderful vacation!



Thank you!

Feliks

732-213-8571

- Call 911 for any other emergencies and please contact us immediately.



Temperature:

- All bedrooms use a split unit AC system, and the living room has its own additional split unit AC, these also work as a heating system. Additional heat can be turned on using the thermostats for baseboard heat, but this a backup and should not be necessary as the split unit system is very powerful. Use the remotes to turn on. Please be advised all units must be switched to the same mode (cool vs heat) for them to work. If you receive an error please ensure that is the case. The cool icon (snowflake) looks very similar to the heat icon (sun), so always good to double check!



- Hot water heater holds 50 gallons. Please space bath and showers accordingly.



FIREPLACE:

- The fireplace is controlled with dial on the front/center of the unit. To turn on the flame simply turn counterclockwise 1-5. To turn off, turn the dial clockwise one to the pilot position. Be careful not to turn too far into the off position as this will turn off the pilot light, which should stay on at all times. 



COMMUNITY AMENITIES:

•You will need the amenity passes to use these, which you will find hanging on the oars by the entrance. It is always a total of 12 of these, please be very careful not to lose them as they are specific to the home and a $175 replacement fee.

• There are two community pools (open memorial day weekend till  labor day weekend) located at 443 Penn Estates Dr, next to the Archies Corner community store.﻿ The daily pool hours are 11:00 am – 7:00 pm swim at your own risk (not always lifeguards), pending weather conditions.

• Athletic fields and courts are right next to the pools and community center as well.

• ﻿There is an additional a swimmable beach lake. If you exit out the door and turn right you just go straight and cant miss the beach lake area on your left, about a 12 min walk or 1min drive from the home. You should also bring the amenity passes mentioned above just in case they check at the lake.



TV:

- Watch TV via LG Internet TV: Use LG remote to turn on TV (it takes 5 secs to come up). Then navigate to the LG TV app, Netflix, or another streaming service of your choice.



QUIET HOURS:

- 11pm to 7am. Please be respectful to neighbors at all times.

Check-out: 11am

===== TEMPLATE 100 (sent 5x | properties: Lakefront Home w/ Hot Tub, Game Room, Deck, Boats, Fire Pit; Poconos Lakefront with Hot Tub, boats, and more!)
Hey Agnetha, 



We’re so excited to host your stay in the beautiful Poconos! Below you will find check-in instructions as well as some general Information about the home.



Check-in: Dec 27, 2024 at  4:00 PM

Check-out: Dec 29, 2024 at 11:00 AM





We have guests checking in on Dec 29, 2024, so we ask that you please adhere to the 11:00 AM checkout time. Thanks for your understanding!



Arriving at the community: 



Penn Estates is a gated community with 2 entrances. ALL GUESTS MUST CHECK IN AT THE MAIN GATE , LOCATED AT: 



525 Penn Estates Dr, East Stroudsburg PA, 18301. 



Drive up to gate via the right-side "Visitors" lane, and contact the gatestaff through the button on the machine. The registered guest will need to provide a valid drivers license at check-in. 



Upon check-in you will receive a printed gate pass, which can be used to enter both the front and back gates for the duration of your stay. 



Entry Door Lock: 8550



- To unlock from outside: Tap the Yale button on the door lock. A keypad will appear. Use the pin provided above, and hit “✔︎” to submit the code.



To lock from outside: Tap the "Yale" logo. Make sure it is locked.



Parking:

- Driveway is h-shaped and is on a hill. Be careful and drive slowly up and down the driveway. You can fit up to 6 cars.



DO NOT PARK IN THE STREET.



Wifi:



Name: Lakeside 

Password:  relax484



GUESTS &amp; DELIVERIES: 



All guests must be noted on the registration form. Guests who are not on the form will be denied entry at the gate. 



To allow a food, Uber, or any other delivery driver through the gate, you must send a message via airbnb, and we will submit it into the gate. Gatehouse staff will not allow any driver through without a regstration form or a delivery registration. 



Our general store inside the .community is Archie's Corner (www.archiescorner.com) and is available for food and any last minute needs at 443 Penn Estates drive, next to the pools and community center. We recommend the breakfast sandwich, Italian Hero, and chicken fingers!



HOT TUB: 

- Hot tub is always on and ready to use. 

- Feel free to adjust the temperature as desired using the controls. 

- NO FOOD OR DRINKS IN HOT TUB!

- Please be sure to keep hot tub lid closed when not in use. 

– Please make sure to wash off any lotions or hair gels prior to entering the hot tub, as these will cause chemical imbalances in the water.  – There are individual plastic cups with chlorine powder in them in the cabinet above the kitchen microwave. Drop one of these into the tub after each use to ensure the hot tub stays fresh for your next use.It’s 





Safety:

- Fire Extinguisher is under the sink.

- First Aid Kit is in the labeled cabinet in the kitchen.

- Life Jackets for Kayaks are located in the upstairs closet.

- Call 911 for any other emergencies and please contact us immediately.



Temperature:

- All bedrooms use a split unit AC system, and the living room has its own additional split unit AC, these also work as a heating system. Additional heat can be turned on using the thermostats for baseboard heat, but this a backup and should not be necessary as the split unit system is very powerful. Use the remotes to turn on. Please be advised all units must be switched to the same mode (cool vs heat) for them to work. If you receive an error please ensure that is the case. The cool icon (snowflake) looks very similar to the heat icon (sun), so always good to double check!



- Hot water heater holds 50 gallons. Please space bath and showers accordingly.



FIREPLACE:

- The fireplace is controlled with dial on the front/center of the unit, from 1 to 5. To turn on the flame simply turn counterclockwise, and the higher the number the higher the flame. To turn off, turn the dial clockwise one click past the 1 position. Be careful not to turn too far into the off or pilot position as this will turn off the pilot light, which should stay on at all times. 



COMMUNITY AMENITIES:

•You will need the amenity passes to use these, which you will find hanging on the oars by the entrance. It is always a total of 12 of these, please be very careful not to lose them as they are specific to the home and a $75 replacement fee.

• There are two community pools located at 443 Penn Estates Dr, next to the Archies Corner community store (open memorial day weekend till  labor day weekend).﻿ The daily pool hours are 11:00 am – 7:00 pm swim at your own risk (not always lifeguards), pending weather conditions.

• Athletic fields and courts are right next to the pools and community center as well.

• ﻿There is an additional a swimmable beach lake. If you exit out the door and turn right you just go straight and cant miss the beach lake area on your left, about a 12 min walk or 1min drive from the home. You should also bring the amenity passes mentioned above just in case they check at the lake.



TV:

- Watch TV via LG Internet TV: Use LG remote to turn on TV (it takes 5 secs to come up). Then navigate to the LG TV app, Netflix, or another streaming service of your choice.



QUIET HOURS:

- 11pm to 7am. Please be respectful to neighbors at all times.



TRASH:

All trash should be placed in the bins just outside the garage door, they are mixed use trash and recycling so either works. It is picked up between monday morning and tuesday night directly from where they are, so no need to bring anything to the street. If they are filled up and you are checking out prior to pick up, just place your bags next to the bins and we will take care of it from there.



Check-out: 11am



Please be aware that the cleaning fee is for basic whole house cleaning. Anything out of ordinary (such as excessive trash, unremovable stains, etc) will incur guests extra cleaning fees as per the rental agreement.



- If you have any questions/ issues, feel free to contact us and we will try our best to make your stay as comfortable and pleasant as possible. Enjoy your stay and have a wonderful vacation!



Thank you!

Feliks

Summit Lakeside Rentals

732-213-8571

Hey Brandon, 



We’re so excited to host your stay in the beautiful Poconos! Below you will find check-in instructions as well as some general Information about the home.



Check-in: Jul 19, 2025 at  4:00 PM

Check-out: Jul 26, 2025 at 11:00 AM





We have guests checking in on Jul 26, 2025, so we ask that you please adhere to the 11:00 AM checkout time. Thanks for your understanding!



Arriving at the community: 



Penn Estates is a gated community with 2 entrances. ALL GUESTS MUST CHECK IN AT THE MAIN GATE , LOCATED AT: 



525 Penn Estates Dr, East Stroudsburg PA, 18301.



This is at Penn Estates Dr and Hallet Rd. Make sure your directions don’t take you through the back gate to get there (Penn Estates Dr and Cranburry Rd) as entry will not be permitted that way.



Drive up to gate via the right-side "Visitors" lane, and contact the gatestaff through the button on the machine. The registered guest will need to provide a valid drivers license at check-in. 



Upon check-in you will receive a printed gate pass, which can be used to enter both the front and back gates for the duration of your stay.



Do not share gate passes or sneak additional vehicles or guests that haven’t been registered. I can not emohasize this enough: they have automatic cameras, security will catch you, and you will recieve an unreasonably high citation. Let’s follow the rules and avoid this please!



Entry Door Lock: 



To unlock from outside, the code to the door is 8550. Enter the code and press the bottom-left "unlock" button. 



Parking:

- Driveway is wide but has a narrow entrance, please be careful not to drive into the culvert to the left and right of the driveway. 



Parking on the gravel to the left of the paved driveway is permitted.  You can fit up to 6 cars total.



DO NOT PARK IN THE STREET.



Wifi:



Name:  Lakeside Manor - 5G

Password:  relax424



Safety:

- Fire Extinguisher is under the sink.

- First Aid Kit is in the labeled cabinet in the kitchen.

- Life Jackets for Kayaks are located in the front entrance closet.

- Call 911 for any other emergencies and please contact us immediately.



Temperature:

- The home is equipped with central heating and air conditioning.

- Please use the Nest Thermostat in the dining room to set your desired temperature. Swipe your finger up and down the right side of the Nest to adjust. 

- The game room heater is turned on via the timer in the far corner to the left of the door, inside the metal switch box. It looks complicated as it is an industrial heater setup, but all you need to do is switch to on :) 



- Hot water heater holds 50 gallons. Please space bath and showers accordingly.



HOT TUB: 

- Hot tub is always on and ready to use. 

- Feel free to adjust the temperature as desired using the controls. 

- NO FOOD OR DRINKS IN HOT TUB!

- Please be sure to keep hot tub lid closed when not in use. 

– Please make sure to wash off any lotions or hair gels prior to entering the hot tub, as these will cause chemical imbalances in the water.  – There are individual plastic cups with chlorine powder in them in the cabinet above the kitchen microwave. Please empty one of these into the tub after each use to ensure the hot tub stays fresh for your next use. After adding chrlorine, please wait 1-2 hours before using the tub. 





FIREPLACE:

- Turning On: The gas fireplace is turned on using the thermostat on the wall behind the couch. Set the thermostat above the current room temperature to turn on the fireplace. Fire will start automatically within 60 seconds.

- Turning Off: Turn the thermostat all the way down.



TV:

- Watch TV via LG Internet TV: Use LG remote to turn on TV (it takes 5 secs to come up). Then navigate to the LG TV app, Netflix, or another streaming service of your choice.



GUESTS &amp; DELIVERIES: 



All guests must be noted on the registration form. Guests who are not on the form will be denied entry at the gate. 



To allow a food, Uber, or any other delivery driver through the gate, you must send a message via Airbnb, and we will call them into the gate. Gatehouse staff will not allow any driver through without a regstration form or a delivery call in. 



Our general store inside the community is Archie's Corner (www.archiescorner.com) and is available for food and any last minute needs at 443 Penn Estates drive, next to the pools and community center. We recommend the breakfast sandwich, Italian Hero, and chicken fingers!



COMMUNITY AMENITIES:

•You will need the amenity passes to use these, which you will find hanging on the oars by the entrance. It is always a total of 12 of these, please be very careful not to lose them as they are specific to the home and a $175 replacement fee.

• There are two community pools (open memorial day weekend till  labor day weekend) located at 443 Penn Estates Dr, next to the Archies Corner community store. The daily pool hours are 11:00 am – 7:00 pm swim at your own risk (not always lifeguards), pending weather conditions.

• Athletic fields and courts are right next to the pools and community center as well.

• ﻿There is an additional swimmable beach lake a bit further down. If you exit out the door and turn right you just go straight and cant miss the beach lake area on your left, about a 15 min walk or 1min drive from the home.



CANOES and KAYAKS:

If you exit the home and turn right, the easement entrance to the lake is two homes down on your right. We have a canoe ready for you on a rack at the lake. (the green one with 288C on the label, rack no. TL1). Oars along with 2 kayaks are on the side of the home and life jackets are in the main closet when you enter.



QUIET HOURS:

- 11pm to 7am. Please be respectful to neighbors at all times.



TRASH:

All trash should be placed in the bins just outside the garage door, they are mixed use trash and recycling so either works. It is picked up between monday morning and tuesday night directly from where they are, so no need to bring anything to the street. If they are filled up and you are checking out prior to pick up, just place your bags next to the bins and we will take care of it from there.



Check-out: 11am



Before Checkout:



- Last but not the least… The cleaning fee is for basic whole house cleaning. Anything out of ordinary (such as excessive trash, unremovable stains, etc) will incur guests extra cleaning fees as per the rental agreement. 



- PLEASE CLEAN UP YOUR DOGS POOP FROM BACK YARD!



- If you have any questions/ issues, feel free to contact me. I will try my best to make your stay as comfortable and pleasant as possible. Enjoy your stay and have a wonderful vacation!



Thank you!

525 Penn Estates Dr, East Stroudsburg PA, 18301.

Upon check-in you will receive a printed gate pass, which can be used to enter both the front and back gates for the duration of your stay. 



Entry Door Lock:

- There is a lock box on the ground floor door under the deck. Use  code 8550 to unlock the box and access the door key. If you have trouble, you want to lock halfway before closing so the little latch is partially out, firmly slide the door closed, and lock the rest of the way.



Please return the key to the lockbox anytime you leave the house and venture out. This will ensure you don’t lock yourself out. Losing the key will result in a $50 replacement fee which will be deducted from your deposit.





Parking:

- Driveway is on a hill. Be careful and drive slowly up and down the driveway. You can fit up to 5 cars in a row.



DO NOT PARK IN THE STREET.



Wifi:



Name: The Chalet

Password: relax475



Safety:

- Fire Extinguisher is under the sink.

- First Aid Kit is in the labeled cabinet in the kitchen.

- Life Jackets for Kayaks are located in the upstairs closet.

- Call 911 for any other emergencies and please contact us immediately.



Temperature:

- Each room has its own thermostat for heat that can be adjusted manually with the controls. 

- All rooms are equiped with air conditioning. Please use the white remote on the wall to turn it on and set the desired temperature. In order for the system to work, all rooms must be set to COOL. If one of the rooms is set to HEAT, while the others are set to cool, the system will not function and will display an error message. You can confirm the setting is correct when you see the snowflake icon on the remote LCD screen. 



- Hot water heater holds 50 gallons. Please space bath and showers accordingly.





FIREPLACE:

- Turning On: The gas fireplace is turned on using the small black remote. Press the button once (you will hear a beep) to turn it on. Fire will start automatically within 60 seconds after the beep.

- Turning Off: Press the button once. You will hear two beeps and the fire will turn off.



HOT TUB: 

- Hot tub is always on and ready to use. 

- Feel free to adjust the temperature as desired using the controls. 

- NO FOOD OR DRINKS IN HOT TUB!

- Please be sure to keep hot tub lid closed when not in use. 

– Please make sure to wash off any lotions or hair gels prior to entering the hot tub, as these will cause chemical imbalances in the water.  – There are individual plastic cups with chlorine powder in them in the cabinet above the kitchen microwave. Drop one of these into the tub after each use to ensure the hot tub stays fresh for your next use.



SAUNA:

The sauna is an infrared sauna, that opperates on a 90 minute timer. It takes about 30-45 minutes to get up to a good temperature (most people prefer 120-140), though a bit longer if it is cold outside. Infrared sauna works by heating your body directly, so it may not feel super hot when you first enter but will quickly heat you up once inside. 



TV:

- Watch TV via LG Internet TV: Use LG remote to turn on TV (it takes 5 secs to come up). Then navigate to the LG TV app, Netflix, or another streaming service of your choice.



COMMUNITY AMENITIES:

•You will need the amenity passes to use these, which you will find hanging on the oars by the entrance. It is always a total of 12 of these, please be very careful not to lose them as they are specific to the home and a $75 replacement fee.

• There are two community pools located at 443 Penn Estates Dr, next to the Archies Corner community store (open memorial day weekend till  labor day weekend).﻿ The daily pool hours are 11:00 am – 7:00 pm swim at your own risk (not always lifeguards), pending weather conditions.

• Athletic fields and courts are right next to the pools and community center as well.

• ﻿There is also a swimmable beach lake. If you exit out the door and turn left you just go straight and cant miss the beach lake area on your left, about a 12 min walk or 1min drive from the home. You should also bring the amenity passes mentioned above just in case they check at the lake.



CANOES and KAYAKS:

If you exit the home and turn right, the easement entrance to the lake is two homes down on your left. We have a canoe ready for you on a rack at the lake. (the red one with 81C on the label, rack no. TL4 on the bottom). Oars and a kayak are on the front of the home and life jackets are in the upstairs closet. Please make sure to return all after use.





QUIET HOURS:

- 11pm to 7am. Please be respectful to neighbors at all times.



TRASH:

All trash should be placed in the bins just outside the garage door, they are mixed use trash and recycling so either works. It is picked up between monday morning and tuesday night directly from where they are, so no need to bring anything to the street. If they are filled up and you are checking out prior to pick up, just place your bags next to the bins and we will take care of it from there.



GUESTS &amp; DELIVERIES: 



All guests must be noted on the registration form. Guests who are not on the form will be denied entry at the gate. 



To allow a food, Uber, or any other delivery driver through the gate, you must send a message via Airbnb, and we will call them into the gate. Gatehouse staff will not allow any driver through without a regstration form or a delivery call in. 



Our general store inside the .community is Archie's Corner (www.archiescorner.com) and is available for food and any last minute needs at 443 Penn Estates drive, next to the pools and community center. We recommend the breakfast sandwich, Italian Hero, and chicken fingers!



Check-out: 11am

Arriving at the community: 



Penn Estates is a gated community with 2 entrances. ALL GUESTS MUST CHECK IN AT THE MAIN GATE , LOCATED AT: 



525 Penn Estates Dr, East Stroudsburg PA, 18301. 



Drive up to gate via the right-side "Visitors" lane, and contact the gatestaff through the button on the machine. The registered guest will need to provide a valid drivers license at check-in. 



Upon check-in you will receive a printed gate pass, which can be used to enter both the front and back gates for the duration of your stay. 



Entry Door Lock:

- There is a lock box on the ground floor door under the deck. Use  code 8550 to unlock the box and access the door key. If you have trouble, you want to lock halfway before closing so the little latch is partially out, firmly slide the door closed, and lock the rest of the way.



Please return the key to the lockbox anytime you leave the house and venture out. This will ensure you don’t lock yourself out. Losing the key will result in a $50 replacement fee which will be deducted from your deposit.





Parking:

- Driveway is on a hill. Be careful and drive slowly up and down the driveway. You can fit up to 5 cars in a row.



DO NOT PARK IN THE STREET.



Wifi:



Name: The Chalet

Password: relax475



Safety:

- Fire Extinguisher is under the sink.

- First Aid Kit is in the labeled cabinet in the kitchen.

- Life Jackets for Kayaks are located in the upstairs closet.

- Call 911 for any other emergencies and please contact us immediately.



Temperature:

- Each room has its own thermostat for heat that can be adjusted manually with the controls. 

- All rooms are equiped with air conditioning. Please use the white remote on the wall to turn it on and set the desired temperature. In order for the system to work, all rooms must be set to COOL. If one of the rooms is set to HEAT, while the others are set to cool, the system will not function and will display an error message. You can confirm the setting is correct when you see the snowflake icon on the remote LCD screen. 



- Hot water heater holds 50 gallons. Please space bath and showers accordingly.





FIREPLACE:

- Turning On: The gas fireplace is turned on using the small black remote. Press the button once (you will hear a beep) to turn it on. Fire will start automatically within 60 seconds after the beep.

- Turning Off: Press the button once. You will hear two beeps and the fire will turn off.



HOT TUB: 

- Hot tub is always on and ready to use. 

- Feel free to adjust the temperature as desired using the controls. 

- NO FOOD OR DRINKS IN HOT TUB!

- Please be sure to keep hot tub lid closed when not in use. 

– Please make sure to wash off any lotions or hair gels prior to entering the hot tub, as these will cause chemical imbalances in the water.  – There are individual plastic cups with chlorine powder in them in the cabinet above the kitchen microwave. Drop one of these into the tub after each use to ensure the hot tub stays fresh for your next use.



SAUNA:

The sauna is an infrared sauna, that opperates on a 90 minute timer. It takes about 30-45 minutes to get up to a good temperature (most people prefer 120-140), though a bit longer if it is cold outside. Infrared sauna works by heating your body directly, so it may not feel super hot when you first enter but will quickly heat you up once inside. 



TV:

- Watch TV via LG Internet TV: Use LG remote to turn on TV (it takes 5 secs to come up). Then navigate to the LG TV app, Netflix, or another streaming service of your choice.



COMMUNITY AMENITIES:

• There are two community pools located at 443 Penn Estates Dr, next to the Archies Corner community store (open memorial day weekend till  labor day weekend).﻿ The daily pool hours are 11:00 am – 7:00 pm swim at your own risk (not always lifeguards), pending weather conditions.

• Athletic fields and courts are right next to the pools and community center as well.

Please make sure to return all after use.

Additional heat can be turned on using the thermostats for baseboard heat, but this a backup and should not be necessary as the split unit system is very powerful. Use the remotes to turn on. Please be advised all units must be switched to the same mode (cool vs heat) for them to work. If you receive an error please ensure that is the case. The cool icon (snowflake) looks very similar to the heat icon (sun), so always good to double check!



- Hot water heater holds 50 gallons. Please space bath and showers accordingly.



FIREPLACE:

- The fireplace is controlled with dial on the front/center of the unit. To turn on the flame simply turn counterclockwise 1-5. To turn off, turn the dial clockwise one to the pilot position. Be careful not to turn too far into the off position as this will turn off the pilot light, which should stay on at all times. 



COMMUNITY AMENITIES:

•You will need the amenity passes to use these, which you will find hanging on the oars by the entrance. It is always a total of 12 of these, please be very careful not to lose them as they are specific to the home and a $175 replacement fee.

• There are two community pools (open memorial day weekend till  labor day weekend) located at 443 Penn Estates Dr, next to the Archies Corner community store.﻿ The daily pool hours are 11:00 am – 7:00 pm swim at your own risk (not always lifeguards), pending weather conditions.

• Athletic fields and courts are right next to the pools and community center as well.

• ﻿There is an additional a swimmable beach lake. If you exit out the door and turn right you just go straight and cant miss the beach lake area on your left, about a 12 min walk or 1min drive from the home. You should also bring the amenity passes mentioned above just in case they check at the lake.



TV:

- Watch TV via LG Internet TV: Use LG remote to turn on TV (it takes 5 secs to come up). Then navigate to the LG TV app, Netflix, or another streaming service of your choice.



QUIET HOURS:

- 11pm to 7am. Please be respectful to neighbors at all times.



TRASH:

All trash should be placed in the bins just outside the garage door, they are mixed use trash and recycling so either works. It is picked up between monday morning and tuesday night directly from where they are, so no need to bring anything to the street. If they are filled up and you are checking out prior to pick up, just place your bags next to the bins and we will take care of it from there.



Check-out: 11am



Please be aware that the cleaning fee is for basic whole house cleaning. Anything out of ordinary (such as excessive trash, unremovable stains, etc) will incur guests extra cleaning fees as per the rental agreement.



- If you have any questions/ issues, feel free to contact us and we will try our best to make your stay as comfortable and pleasant as possible. Enjoy your stay and have a wonderful vacation!



Thank you!

HOT TUB:

SAUNA:

The sauna is an infrared sauna, that opperates on a 90 minute timer. It takes about 30-45 minutes to get up to a good temperature (most people prefer 120-140), though a bit longer if it is cold outside. Infrared sauna works by heating your body directly, so it may not feel super hot when you first enter but will quickly heat you up once inside. 



TV:

It is always a total of 12 of these, please be very careful not to lose them as they are specific to the home and a $75 replacement fee. The daily pool hours are 11:00 am – 7:00 pm swim at your own risk (not always lifeguards), pending weather conditions.



CANOES and KAYAKS:

If you exit the home and turn right, the easement entrance to the lake is two homes down on your left. We have a canoe ready for you on a rack at the lake. Temperature:

- All bedrooms use a split unit AC system, and the living room has its own additional split unit AC, these also work as a heating system. Additional heat can be turned on using the thermostats for baseboard heat, but this a backup and should not be necessary as the split unit system is very powerful. Use the remotes to turn on. Please be advised all units must be switched to the same mode (cool vs heat) for them to work. If you receive an error please ensure that is the case. The cool icon (snowflake) looks very similar to the heat icon (sun), so always good to double check!



- Hot water heater holds 50 gallons. Please space bath and showers accordingly.



FIREPLACE:

- The fireplace is controlled with dial on the front/center of the unit. To turn on the flame simply turn counterclockwise 1-5. To turn off, turn the dial clockwise one to the pilot position. Be careful not to turn too far into the off position as this will turn off the pilot light, which should stay on at all times. 



COMMUNITY AMENITIES:

This is at Penn Estates Dr and Hallet Rd. Make sure your directions don’t take you through the back gate to get there (Penn Estates Dr and Cranburry Rd) as entry will not be permitted that way.



Drive up to gate via the right-side "Visitors" lane, and contact the gatestaff through the button on the machine. The registered guest will need to provide a valid drivers license at check-in. 



Upon check-in you will receive a printed gate pass, which can be used to enter both the front and back gates for the duration of your stay.



Do not share gate passes or sneak additional vehicles or guests that haven’t been registered. I can not emohasize this enough: they have automatic cameras, security will catch you, and you will recieve an unreasonably high citation. Let’s follow the rules and avoid this please!



Entry Door Lock: 



To unlock from outside, the code to the door is 8550. Enter the code and press the bottom-left "unlock" button. 



Parking:

- Driveway is wide but has a narrow entrance, please be careful not to drive into the culvert to the left and right of the driveway. 



Parking on the gravel to the left of the paved driveway is permitted.  You can fit up to 6 cars total.



DO NOT PARK IN THE STREET.



Wifi:



Name:  Lakeside Manor - 5G

Password:  relax424



Safety:

- Fire Extinguisher is under the sink.

- First Aid Kit is in the labeled cabinet in the kitchen.

- Life Jackets for Kayaks are located in the front entrance closet.

- Call 911 for any other emergencies and please contact us immediately.



Temperature:

- The home is equipped with central heating and air conditioning.

- Please use the Nest Thermostat in the dining room to set your desired temperature. Swipe your finger up and down the right side of the Nest to adjust. 

- The game room heater is turned on via the timer in the far corner to the left of the door, inside the metal switch box. It looks complicated as it is an industrial heater setup, but all you need to do is switch to on :) 



- Hot water heater holds 50 gallons. Please space bath and showers accordingly.



HOT TUB: 

- Hot tub is always on and ready to use. 

- Feel free to adjust the temperature as desired using the controls. 

- NO FOOD OR DRINKS IN HOT TUB!

- Please be sure to keep hot tub lid closed when not in use. 

– Please make sure to wash off any lotions or hair gels prior to entering the hot tub, as these will cause chemical imbalances in the water.  – There are individual plastic cups with chlorine powder in them in the cabinet above the kitchen microwave. Please empty one of these into the tub after each use to ensure the hot tub stays fresh for your next use. After adding chrlorine, please wait 1-2 hours before using the tub. 





FIREPLACE:

- Turning On: The gas fireplace is turned on using the thermostat on the wall behind the couch. Set the thermostat above the current room temperature to turn on the fireplace. Fire will start automatically within 60 seconds.

- Turning Off: Turn the thermostat all the way down.



TV:

- Watch TV via LG Internet TV: Use LG remote to turn on TV (it takes 5 secs to come up). Then navigate to the LG TV app, Netflix, or another streaming service of your choice.



GUESTS &amp; DELIVERIES: 



All guests must be noted on the registration form. Guests who are not on the form will be denied entry at the gate. 



To allow a food, Uber, or any other delivery driver through the gate, you must send a message via Airbnb, and we will call them into the gate. Gatehouse staff will not allow any driver through without a regstration form or a delivery call in. 



Our general store inside the community is Archie's Corner (www.archiescorner.com) and is available for food and any last minute needs at 443 Penn Estates drive, next to the pools and community center. We recommend the breakfast sandwich, Italian Hero, and chicken fingers!



COMMUNITY AMENITIES:

•You will need the amenity passes to use these, which you will find hanging on the oars by the entrance. It is always a total of 12 of these, please be very careful not to lose them as they are specific to the home and a $175 replacement fee.

• There are two community pools (open memorial day weekend till  labor day weekend) located at 443 Penn Estates Dr, next to the Archies Corner community store. The daily pool hours are 11:00 am – 7:00 pm swim at your own risk (not always lifeguards), pending weather conditions.

• Athletic fields and courts are right next to the pools and community center as well.

• ﻿There is an additional swimmable beach lake a bit further down. If you exit out the door and turn right you just go straight and cant miss the beach lake area on your left, about a 15 min walk or 1min drive from the home.



CANOES and KAYAKS:

If you exit the home and turn right, the easement entrance to the lake is two homes down on your right. We have a canoe ready for you on a rack at the lake. (the green one with 288C on the label, rack no. TL1). Oars along with 2 kayaks are on the side of the home and life jackets are in the main closet when you enter.



QUIET HOURS:

- 11pm to 7am. Please be respectful to neighbors at all times.



TRASH:

All trash should be placed in the bins just outside the garage door, they are mixed use trash and recycling so either works. It is picked up between monday morning and tuesday night directly from where they are, so no need to bring anything to the street. If they are filled up and you are checking out prior to pick up, just place your bags next to the bins and we will take care of it from there.



Check-out: 11am



Before Checkout:



- Last but not the least… The cleaning fee is for basic whole house cleaning. Anything out of ordinary (such as excessive trash, unremovable stains, etc) will incur guests extra cleaning fees as per the rental agreement. 



- PLEASE CLEAN UP YOUR DOGS POOP FROM BACK YARD!



- If you have any questions/ issues, feel free to contact me. I will try my best to make your stay as comfortable and pleasant as possible. Enjoy your stay and have a wonderful vacation!



Thank you!

Feliks

Entry Door Lock:

- There is a lock box on the ground floor door under the deck. Use  code 8550 to unlock the box and access the door key. If you have trouble, you want to lock halfway before closing so the little latch is partially out, firmly slide the door closed, and lock the rest of the way.

Temperature:

- Each room has its own thermostat for heat that can be adjusted manually with the controls. 

- All rooms are equiped with air conditioning. Please use the white remote on the wall to turn it on and set the desired temperature. In order for the system to work, all rooms must be set to COOL. If one of the rooms is set to HEAT, while the others are set to cool, the system will not function and will display an error message. You can confirm the setting is correct when you see the snowflake icon on the remote LCD screen. 



- Hot water heater holds 50 gallons. Please space bath and showers accordingly.





FIREPLACE:

- Turning Off: Press the button once. You will hear two beeps and the fire will turn off.



HOT TUB:

Drop one of these into the tub after each use to ensure the hot tub stays fresh for your next use.



SAUNA:

The sauna is an infrared sauna, that opperates on a 90 minute timer. It takes about 30-45 minutes to get up to a good temperature (most people prefer 120-140), though a bit longer if it is cold outside. Infrared sauna works by heating your body directly, so it may not feel super hot when you first enter but will quickly heat you up once inside.

Upon check-in you will receive a printed gate pass, which can be used to enter both the front and back gates for the duration of your stay.



Do not share gate passes or sneak additional vehicles or guests that haven’t been registered. I can not emohasize this enough: they have automatic cameras, security will catch you, and you will recieve an unreasonably high citation. Let’s follow the rules and avoid this please!



Entry Door Lock:

- There is a lock box on the ground floor door under the deck. Use  code 8550 to unlock the box and access the door key. If you have trouble, you want to lock halfway before closing so the little latch is partially out, firmly slide the door closed, and lock the rest of the way.



Please return the key to the lockbox anytime you leave the house and venture out. This will ensure you don’t lock yourself out. Losing the key will result in a $50 replacement fee which will be deducted from your deposit.





Parking:

- Driveway is on a hill. Be careful and drive slowly up and down the driveway. You can fit up to 5 cars in a row.



DO NOT PARK IN THE STREET.



Wifi:



Name: The Chalet

Password: relax475



Safety:

- Fire Extinguisher is under the sink.

- First Aid Kit is in the labeled cabinet in the kitchen.

- Life Jackets for Kayaks are located in the upstairs closet.

- Call 911 for any other emergencies and please contact us immediately.



Temperature:

- Each room has its own thermostat for heat that can be adjusted manually with the controls. 

- All rooms are equiped with air conditioning. Please use the white remote on the wall to turn it on and set the desired temperature. In order for the system to work, all rooms must be set to COOL. If one of the rooms is set to HEAT, while the others are set to cool, the system will not function and will display an error message. You can confirm the setting is correct when you see the snowflake icon on the remote LCD screen. 



- Hot water heater holds 50 gallons. Please space bath and showers accordingly.





FIREPLACE:

- Turning On: The gas fireplace is turned on using the small black remote. Press the button once (you will hear a beep) to turn it on. Fire will start automatically within 60 seconds after the beep.

- Turning Off: Press the button once. You will hear two beeps and the fire will turn off.



HOT TUB: 

- Hot tub is always on and ready to use. 

- Feel free to adjust the temperature as desired using the controls. 

- NO FOOD OR DRINKS IN HOT TUB!

- Please be sure to keep hot tub lid closed when not in use. 

– Please make sure to wash off any lotions or hair gels prior to entering the hot tub, as these will cause chemical imbalances in the water.  – There are individual plastic cups with chlorine powder in them in the cabinet above the kitchen microwave. Drop one of these into the tub after each use to ensure the hot tub stays fresh for your next use.



SAUNA:

The sauna is an infrared sauna, that opperates on a 90 minute timer. It takes about 30-45 minutes to get up to a good temperature (most people prefer 120-140), though a bit longer if it is cold outside. Infrared sauna works by heating your body directly, so it may not feel super hot when you first enter but will quickly heat you up once inside. 



TV:

- Watch TV via LG Internet TV: Use LG remote to turn on TV (it takes 5 secs to come up). Then navigate to the LG TV app, Netflix, or another streaming service of your choice.



COMMUNITY AMENITIES:

•You will need the amenity passes to use these, which you will find hanging on the oars by the entrance. It is always a total of 12 of these, please be very careful not to lose them as they are specific to the home and a $175 replacement fee.

• There are two community pools (open memorial day weekend till  labor day weekend) located at 443 Penn Estates Dr, next to the Archies Corner community store.﻿ The daily pool hours are 11:00 am – 7:00 pm swim at your own risk (not always lifeguards), pending weather conditions.

• Athletic fields and courts are right next to the pools and community center as well.

• ﻿There is also a swimmable beach lake. If you exit out the door and turn left you just go straight and cant miss the beach lake area on your left, about a 12 min walk or 1min drive from the home. You should also bring the amenity passes mentioned above just in case they check at the lake.



CANOES and KAYAKS:

If you exit the home and turn right, the easement entrance to the lake is two homes down on your left. We have a canoe ready for you on a rack at the lake. (the red one with 81C on the label, rack no. TL4 on the bottom). Oars and a kayak are on the front of the home and life jackets are in the upstairs closet. Please make sure to return all after use.





QUIET HOURS:

- 11pm to 7am. Please be respectful to neighbors at all times.



TRASH:

All trash should be placed in the bins just outside the garage door, they are mixed use trash and recycling so either works. It is picked up between monday morning and tuesday night directly from where they are, so no need to bring anything to the street. If they are filled up and you are checking out prior to pick up, just place your bags next to the bins and we will take care of it from there.



GUESTS &amp; DELIVERIES: 



All guests must be noted on the registration form. Guests who are not on the form will be denied entry at the gate. 



To allow a food, Uber, or any other delivery driver through the gate, you must send a message via Airbnb, and we will call them into the gate. Gatehouse staff will not allow any driver through without a regstration form or a delivery call in. 



Our general store inside the community is Archie's Corner (www.archiescorner.com) and is available for food and any last minute needs at 443 Penn Estates drive, next to the pools and community center. We recommend the breakfast sandwich, Italian Hero, and chicken fingers!



Check-out: 11am



The cleaning fee is for basic whole house cleaning. Anything out of ordinary (such as excessive trash, unremovable stains, etc) will incur guests extra cleaning fees as per the rental agreement.



- If you have any questions/ issues, feel free to contact me. I will try my best to make your stay as comfortable and pleasant as possible. Enjoy your stay and have a wonderful vacation!



Thank you!
